\DoxyCodeLine{522   \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{523     \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} ((q31\_t) (x >> 32) != ((q31\_t) x >> 31)) ?}
\DoxyCodeLine{524       ((0x7FFFFFFF \string^ ((q31\_t) (x >> 63)))) : (q31\_t) x;}
\DoxyCodeLine{525   \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{526 }

\DoxyCodeLine{534       ((0x7FFF \string^ ((q15\_t) (x >> 63)))) : (q15\_t) (x >> 15);}
\DoxyCodeLine{535   \}}

\DoxyCodeLine{573   CMSIS\_INLINE \_\_STATIC\_INLINE uint32\_t arm\_recip\_q31(}
\DoxyCodeLine{574   q31\_t in,}
\DoxyCodeLine{575   q31\_t * dst,}
\DoxyCodeLine{576   q31\_t * pRecipTable)}
\DoxyCodeLine{577   \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{578     q31\_t out;}
\DoxyCodeLine{579     uint32\_t tempVal;}
\DoxyCodeLine{580     uint32\_t index, i;}
\DoxyCodeLine{581     uint32\_t signBits;}
\DoxyCodeLine{582 }
\DoxyCodeLine{583     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (in > 0)}
\DoxyCodeLine{584     \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{585       signBits = ((uint32\_t) (\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_m_s_i_s___core___instruction_interface_ga5d5bb1527e042be4a9fa5a33f65cc248}{\_\_CLZ}}( in) -\/ 1));}
\DoxyCodeLine{586     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{587     \textcolor{keywordflow}{else}}
\DoxyCodeLine{588     \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{589       signBits = ((uint32\_t) (\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_m_s_i_s___core___instruction_interface_ga5d5bb1527e042be4a9fa5a33f65cc248}{\_\_CLZ}}(-\/in) -\/ 1));}
\DoxyCodeLine{590     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{591 }
\DoxyCodeLine{592     \textcolor{comment}{/* Convert input sample to 1.31 format */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{593     in = (in << signBits);}
\DoxyCodeLine{594 }
\DoxyCodeLine{595     \textcolor{comment}{/* calculation of index for initial approximated Val */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{596     index = (uint32\_t)(in >> 24);}
\DoxyCodeLine{597     index = (index \& INDEX\_MASK);}
\DoxyCodeLine{598 }
\DoxyCodeLine{599     \textcolor{comment}{/* 1.31 with exp 1 */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{600     out = pRecipTable[index];}
\DoxyCodeLine{601 }
\DoxyCodeLine{602     \textcolor{comment}{/* calculation of reciprocal value */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{603     \textcolor{comment}{/* running approximation for two iterations */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{604     \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (i = 0U; i < 2U; i++)}
\DoxyCodeLine{605     \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{606       tempVal = (uint32\_t) (((q63\_t) in * out) >> 31);}
\DoxyCodeLine{607       tempVal = 0x7FFFFFFFu -\/ tempVal;}
\DoxyCodeLine{608       \textcolor{comment}{/*      1.31 with exp 1 */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{609       \textcolor{comment}{/* out = (q31\_t) (((q63\_t) out * tempVal) >> 30); */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{610       out = clip\_q63\_to\_q31(((q63\_t) out * tempVal) >> 30);}
\DoxyCodeLine{611     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{612 }
\DoxyCodeLine{613     \textcolor{comment}{/* write output */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{614     *dst = out;}
\DoxyCodeLine{615 }
\DoxyCodeLine{616     \textcolor{comment}{/* return num of signbits of out = 1/in value */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{617     \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} (signBits + 1U);}
\DoxyCodeLine{618   \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{619 }
\DoxyCodeLine{620 }
\DoxyCodeLine{624   CMSIS\_INLINE \_\_STATIC\_INLINE uint32\_t arm\_recip\_q15(}
\DoxyCodeLine{625   q15\_t in,}
\DoxyCodeLine{626   q15\_t * dst,}
\DoxyCodeLine{627   q15\_t * pRecipTable)}
\DoxyCodeLine{628   \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{629     q15\_t out = 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{630     uint32\_t tempVal = 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{631     uint32\_t index = 0, i = 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{632     uint32\_t signBits = 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{633 }
\DoxyCodeLine{634     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (in > 0)}
\DoxyCodeLine{635     \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{636       signBits = ((uint32\_t)(\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_m_s_i_s___core___instruction_interface_ga5d5bb1527e042be4a9fa5a33f65cc248}{\_\_CLZ}}( in) -\/ 17));}
\DoxyCodeLine{637     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{638     \textcolor{keywordflow}{else}}
\DoxyCodeLine{639     \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{640       signBits = ((uint32\_t)(\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_m_s_i_s___core___instruction_interface_ga5d5bb1527e042be4a9fa5a33f65cc248}{\_\_CLZ}}(-\/in) -\/ 17));}
\DoxyCodeLine{641     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{642 }
\DoxyCodeLine{643     \textcolor{comment}{/* Convert input sample to 1.15 format */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{644     in = (in << signBits);}
\DoxyCodeLine{645 }
\DoxyCodeLine{646     \textcolor{comment}{/* calculation of index for initial approximated Val */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{647     index = (uint32\_t)(in >>  8);}
\DoxyCodeLine{648     index = (index \& INDEX\_MASK);}
\DoxyCodeLine{649 }
\DoxyCodeLine{650     \textcolor{comment}{/*      1.15 with exp 1  */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{651     out = pRecipTable[index];}
\DoxyCodeLine{652 }
\DoxyCodeLine{653     \textcolor{comment}{/* calculation of reciprocal value */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{654     \textcolor{comment}{/* running approximation for two iterations */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{655     \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (i = 0U; i < 2U; i++)}
\DoxyCodeLine{656     \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{657       tempVal = (uint32\_t) (((q31\_t) in * out) >> 15);}
\DoxyCodeLine{658       tempVal = 0x7FFFu -\/ tempVal;}
\DoxyCodeLine{659       \textcolor{comment}{/*      1.15 with exp 1 */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{660       out = (q15\_t) (((q31\_t) out * tempVal) >> 14);}
\DoxyCodeLine{661       \textcolor{comment}{/* out = clip\_q31\_to\_q15(((q31\_t) out * tempVal) >> 14); */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{662     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{663 }
\DoxyCodeLine{664     \textcolor{comment}{/* write output */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{665     *dst = out;}
\DoxyCodeLine{666 }
\DoxyCodeLine{667     \textcolor{comment}{/* return num of signbits of out = 1/in value */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{668     \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} (signBits + 1);}
\DoxyCodeLine{669   \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{670 }

\DoxyCodeLine{6753     \}}

\DoxyCodeLine{6756     index = (xIndex -\/ 1) + (yIndex -\/ 1) * S-\/>\mbox{\hyperlink{structarm__bilinear__interp__instance__f32_aede17bebfb1f835b61d71dd813eab3f8}{numCols}};}

\DoxyCodeLine{6763     \textcolor{comment}{/* Calculation of index for two nearest points in Y-\/direction */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6764     index = (xIndex -\/ 1) + (yIndex) * S-\/>\mbox{\hyperlink{structarm__bilinear__interp__instance__f32_aede17bebfb1f835b61d71dd813eab3f8}{numCols}};}

\DoxyCodeLine{6767     \textcolor{comment}{/* Read two nearest points in Y-\/direction */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6768     f10 = pData[index];}
\DoxyCodeLine{6769     f11 = pData[index + 1];}
\DoxyCodeLine{6770 }
\DoxyCodeLine{6771     \textcolor{comment}{/* Calculation of intermediate values */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6772     b1 = f00;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6773     b2 = f01 -\/ f00;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6774     b3 = f10 -\/ f00;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6775     b4 = f00 -\/ f01 -\/ f10 + f11;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6776 }
\DoxyCodeLine{6777     \textcolor{comment}{/* Calculation of fractional part in X */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6778     xdiff = X -\/ xIndex;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6779 }

\DoxyCodeLine{6781     ydiff = Y -\/ yIndex;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6782 }
\DoxyCodeLine{6783     \textcolor{comment}{/* Calculation of bi-\/linear interpolated output */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6784     out = b1 + b2 * xdiff + b3 * ydiff + b4 * xdiff * ydiff;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6785 }
\DoxyCodeLine{6786     \textcolor{comment}{/* return to application */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6787     \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} (out);}

\DoxyCodeLine{6932     acc += ((q63\_t) out * (yfract));}

\DoxyCodeLine{6934     \textcolor{comment}{/* y2 * (xfract) * (yfract)  in 1.51 and adding to acc */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6935     out = (q31\_t) (((q63\_t) y2 * (xfract)) >> 4U);}
\DoxyCodeLine{6936     acc += ((q63\_t) out * (yfract));}
\DoxyCodeLine{6937 }
\DoxyCodeLine{6938     \textcolor{comment}{/* acc is in 13.51 format and down shift acc by 36 times */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6939     \textcolor{comment}{/* Convert out to 1.15 format */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6940     \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} ((q15\_t)(acc >> 36));}
\DoxyCodeLine{6941   \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6942 }
